behavior find_clothes_shirt_2158_around_ironing_board_2144(clothes_shirt:item):
    goal: not unknown(clothes_shirt)
    body:
        assert is_clothes_shirt(clothes_shirt)
        bind ironing_board_instance:item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board_instance) and id[ironing_board_instance]==2144
        achieve close_char(char,ironing_board_instance)
        if can_open(ironing_board_instance):
            achieve_once open(ironing_board_instance)
            exp(clothes_shirt,ironing_board_instance)
        else:
            exp(clothes_shirt,ironing_board_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[clothes_shirt]=False
        close[clothes_shirt,ironing_board_instance]=True
        close[ironing_board_instance,clothes_shirt]=True

#goal_representation
 
def is_ironed(item: item):
    # Check if the item is ironed
    return not dirty(item)

behavior iron_clothes(item: item, iron: item, ironing_board: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inhand(item)
        achieve inside(item, ironing_board)
        # Place the item on the ironing board

        achieve_once inhand(iron)
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is on

        achieve_once clean(item)
        # Iron the item to clean it

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        # Select the shirt

        bind skirt: item where:
            is_clothes_skirt(skirt)
        # Select the skirt

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        # Select the iron

        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board)
        # Select the ironing board

        if not is_ironed(shirt):
            iron_clothes(shirt, iron, ironing_board)
        
        if not is_ironed(skirt):
            iron_clothes(skirt, iron, ironing_board)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
behavior iron_clothes(iron: item, clothes: item):
    body:
        achieve plugged(iron)
        # Ensure the iron is plugged in
        achieve is_on(iron)
        # Turn on the iron
        achieve close_char(char, clothes)
        # Assume the character is close to the clothes to iron them

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron)
        # Select the iron

        bind shirt: item where:
            is_clothes_shirt(shirt)
        # Select the shirt

        bind skirt: item where:
            is_clothes_skirt(skirt)
        # Select the skirt

        iron_clothes(iron, shirt)
        iron_clothes(iron, skirt)
#goal_representation_end

def does_basket_have_shirt_or_skirt(basket: item):
    # Check if a basket contains a shirt or a skirt
    symbol has_clothes=exists o: item : (is_clothes_shirt(o) or is_clothes_skirt(o)) and inside(o, basket)
    return has_clothes

behavior locate_shirt_and_skirt():
    body:
        bind dining_room: item where:
            is_dining_room(dining_room)
        # Select the dining room

        if exists basket: item : is_basket_for_clothes(basket) and inside(basket, dining_room) and does_basket_have_shirt_or_skirt(basket):
            # Check if a basket with a shirt or skirt exists inside the dining room
            bind basket: item where:
                is_basket_for_clothes(basket) and inside(basket, dining_room) and does_basket_have_shirt_or_skirt(basket)
            achieve close_char(char, basket)
            # Move towards the basket with clothing inside in the dining room

        else:
            # If no basket with the relevant clothes is found inside the dining room, start inspecting all unvisited baskets
            foreach basket: item:
                if is_basket_for_clothes(basket) and not visited(basket):
                    observe(basket, "Check if there are clothes_shirt_2158 or clothes_skirt_2162 in the basket")
                    # Observe to see if the basket contains the required shirt or skirt

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        locate_shirt_and_skirt()

            # If a basket containing the shirt and skirt is found, approach it

                is_basket_for_clothes(basket) and locate_clothes_in_basket(basket)
            achieve close_char(char, basket)

        else:
            # If not yet found, check all unvisited baskets
            foreach basket: item:
                if is_basket_for_clothes(basket) and not visited(basket):
                    observe(basket, "Check if there is a shirt and a skirt in the basket")

def locate_clothes_in_basket(basket: item):
    symbol has_clothes = exists o: item : (is_clothes_shirt(o) or is_clothes_skirt(o)) and inside(o, basket)
    return has_clothes

behavior __goal__():
    body:

def check_if_iron_is_ready(iron:item):
    symbol is_ready=exists item:item: is_iron(item) and is_on(item) and plugged(item) and id[item]==iron
    return is_ready

behavior iron_clothes(clothes:item, ironing_board:item, iron:item):
    body:
        achieve on(clothes, ironing_board)
        achieve clean(clothes)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind ironing_board: item where:
            is_ironing_board(ironing_board) and id[ironing_board] == 2144
        # Select the ironing board with ID 2144

        bind basket_for_clothes: item where:
            is_basket_for_clothes(basket_for_clothes) and id[basket_for_clothes] == 2078
        # Select the basket for clothes with ID 2078

        bind iron: item where:
            is_iron(iron) and id[iron] == 2161
        # Ensure the iron is prepared for use

        if not check_if_iron_is_ready(iron):
            observe(iron, "Check if the iron is plugged in and turned on")

        foreach clothes: item:
        # Iron all clothes that are in the basket
            if (is_clothes_shirt(clothes) or is_clothes_skirt(clothes)) and inside(clothes, basket_for_clothes):
                iron_clothes(clothes, ironing_board, iron)
